msg:Located at the front of the Wuhan expo center are the intercontinental and Holiday Inn hotels. A good location for a river view and relaxing weekend.

I chose the intercontinental, as our experiences at the Shanghai Wonderland and Chongqing Raffles intercontinental had been fantastic. So I booked this for our anniversary with high expectations. 

The hotel is grand and the rooms are lovely. The lobby cafe where breakfast is served is huge with a venetian style interior and roof. 

The hotel restaurant serves Cantonese style food and is worth a visit. A few photos attached. The service at the restaurant was sub par, and the bill was wrong, which we got the pleasure of finding out when the restaurant began to ring our room repeatedly around 10pm to ask me to go back and pay 30Yuan extra. Which wasn't a problem, but after 4/5 calls late at night to be told I'd walked out without paying down the phone was disappointing when I paid the bill I had been presented with. 

On our a trip we were quite disappointed to find out on arrival that the swimming area was completely closed, as this would have been useful information before booking. 

Our trip to Wuhan was great, but the service at this intercontinental didn't live up to their colleagues and previous experiences.

info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Business travelers
info:146 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted October 16, 2023
msg:Intercontinental Hotel Wuhan Studio Suite: Beautiful River View and Yao National Expo

„ÄêJourney Memory„Äë
"In addition to auto shows, Wuhan also often holds various activities, such as the Snooker Open that is being held recently. Whether it is an event or a concert, athletes, celebrities, entertainers... Wuhan hotels are the most popular hotels to stay in, and the first echelon is naturally It‚Äôs Fairmont and Wanda Reign, and the second tier naturally includes InterContinental (O‚ÄôSullivan will be staying here for the next few days).‚Äù
This Intercontinental is served by high-speed Internet. You can call the engineering department to activate it, otherwise the Internet speed will be slower. Deputy Sales Director Wang Qian (Ellen), Sales Yuki, Manager Ma on duty, etc. were all very enthusiastic and professional, leaving a deep impression on people.

„ÄêMember Benefits„Äë
"No administrative treatment."
No 120 yuan meal coupon. I was given two welcome drink coupons, the welcome fruits were plentiful, and the welcome dessert was the same as the one in the suite holiday next to it, but the plates were different.

„ÄêGuest Room Snapshot„Äë
"The hotel suites are divided into 5 types: 115-square-meter one-bedroom suite with river view, 110-square-meter one-bedroom suite (the bathtub in these two types is not embedded in the wall), open suite, open twin suite, open river view twin suite (The latter three are all 80 square meters). Every time I stay, the hotel upgrades me to a corner room, which is an open-plan suite."
You can receive Phoenix, Phoenix News, and Phoenix Movies here, but you can't receive them from Suite Holiday. To prevent cross-infection, disposable bath bags are provided next to the bathtub. The shower room has a top shower, but the Holiday Suite only has a handheld shower head. The detailed decoration in the room highlights local characteristics, such as decorative paintings related to the Revolution of 1911. The room card has two card faces, one is the river view, the bridge view photo outside the executive lounge, and the Yellow Crane Tower. The new gray long-handled umbrella is very delicate. The full-frame floor-to-ceiling windows in the living room and bedroom offer a panoramic view of the river, which is extremely beautiful. The suites on the Intercontinental side have capsule coffee machines, but the suites on the Holiday Inn side do not.

„ÄêBrief description of public area„Äë
"The swimming pool and suites are shared during holidays. It is recommended to go to the G floor from the elevator around room 33 on each floor. If you want to go down from the elevator near room 01, you have to turn down the elevator. "
The swimming pool is open from 7 am to 9 pm. The swimming pool does not have a children's paddling pool like the Sanlitun Intercontinental and Yujiapu Intercontinental, because this place is mainly for business trips and supplemented by family trips. The facilities in the gym are all good and the brands are all big brands; some of the fitness equipment in the suite holiday are not very "healthy". The road from the hotel to the exhibition hall is full of sweet-scented osmanthus, which is refreshing all the way.

„ÄêCatering Overview„Äë
"Breakfast does not have freshly squeezed juices like Guangzhou Poly Intercontinental, but it is better than the first. After all, the price is too cheap, so the price/performance ratio is still very high. "
Whether it is the lobby bar or the all-day restaurant, the floor height is very high, the view is broad, and the mind is relaxed and happy. It is generally designed in the European retro palace style. There is a small children's playground at the end of the restaurant. The meals available in Suite Holidays and InterContinental include (I mean exactly the same, such as brand, taste, etc.): yogurt, hot dry noodles, tofu skin, beef noodles, etc.; the unique dishes in Suite Holidays include: fried potato chips, etc. ; Unique to InterContinental are: chicken legs, rice rolls, etc.

„ÄêFix omissions and omissions„Äë
"Weddings are held here almost every week. It is very lively and joyful. It is large and has nearly 500 guest rooms. It is especially suitable for holding large-scale events."
There are 56 InterContinental hotels in Greater China, one each in the Hong Kong Special Administrative Region and Taiwan Province of China, and 54 in the Mainland. Among them, there are two apartment-type hotels: Chengdu Yanlord and Yujiapu; and 6 resort-type hotels, most of which are located at the seaside and scenic spots. ; 49 are ordinary type and 47 are in **************. In general, InterContinental Wuhan is a very cost-effective hotel among them: cheap (if you are a major customer of the group, the employee negotiates the price, InterContinental is only 100 more expensive than Suite Holiday, obviously InterContinental is more cost-effective), and the scenery is beautiful . There are about 200 Intercontinental hotels in the world, and China accounts for a quarter, which is an extremely important market (this refers to the IC brand, not IHG InterContinental Hotels Group).

The room was in It is relatively large at the same price, and there is a terrace. The fly in the ointment is that there is nothing in the minibar, and the refrigerator is empty. The configuration is Nescafe instant coffee. The hotel breakfast is 100/person in the restaurant. Overall, the hotel is not bad, and the location is slightly On the other hand, it is very convenient to get on the highway, and it is quiet.
